\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Fingerprint sensor driver for ESP32. 

\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md0}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{1. Introduction}{1. Introduction}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md0}
This driver provides an interface for the fingerprint sensor, enabling fingerprint enrollment, matching, and template storage. It is designed for embedded systems using the ESP32 microcontroller, providing an event-\/driven architecture for efficient processing.\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md1}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{1.\+1 Supported Platforms}{1.\+1 Supported Platforms}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md1}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ESP32-\/based development boards
\item ESP-\/\+IDF (Espressif IoT Development Framework)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md2}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{1.\+2 Compiler and Toolchain}{1.\+2 Compiler and Toolchain}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md2}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item GCC (ESP32 toolchain)
\item Compatible with ESP-\/\+IDF v4.\+x or later
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md3}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{1.\+3 Dependencies}{1.\+3 Dependencies}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md3}
This driver requires the following ESP-\/\+IDF components\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily esp\+\_\+log.\+h} – Logging utilities for debugging and event tracking
\item {\ttfamily driver/uart.\+h} – UART driver for serial communication with the fingerprint module
\item {\ttfamily esp\+\_\+err.\+h} – Standard ESP-\/\+IDF error handling
\item {\ttfamily freertos/\+Free\+RTOS.\+h} and {\ttfamily freertos/task.\+h} – Free\+RTOS support for asynchronous processing
\item {\ttfamily string.\+h} – Standard C library for string manipulation
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md4}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{2. Hardware Interface Description}{2. Hardware Interface Description}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md4}
\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md5}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{2.\+1 UART}{2.\+1 UART}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md5}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Default baud rate\+: 57600 bps (8 data bits, 1 stop bit, no parity)
\item Baud rate adjustable\+: 9600 to 115200 bps
\item Direct connection to MCU (3.\+3V) or use RS232 level converter for PC
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md6}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{2.\+2 Connection}{2.\+2 Connection}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md6}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{TX}} → ESP32 GPIO18
\item {\bfseries{RX}} → ESP32 GPIO17
\item {\bfseries{VCC}} → 3.\+3V
\item {\bfseries{GND}} → GND
\item {\bfseries{INT}} → ESP32 GPIO15
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md7}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{3. Event-\/driven System}{3. Event-\/driven System}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md7}
This system operates on an event-\/driven architecture where each key operation, such as image capture, feature extraction, or match status, triggers specific events. The events help the application know when an operation is complete or has failed. The following events are generated based on the corresponding system actions.\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md8}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{3.\+1 Event Handler}{3.\+1 Event Handler}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md8}
Event handler for processing fingerprint events.

This function processes various fingerprint-\/related events and logs messages based on the event type. It can be used as a sample for handling fingerprint events in the application. The events are processed based on the {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5ae}{fingerprint\+\_\+event\+\_\+type\+\_\+t}} enumeration, and corresponding messages are logged using the ESP-\/\+IDF logging system.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em event} & The fingerprint event that occurred. This can be one of the following\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+FINGER\+\_\+\+DETECTED}\+: Triggered when a finger is detected.
\item {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+IMAGE\+\_\+\+CAPTURED}\+: Triggered when the fingerprint image is captured successfully.
\item {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+EXTRACTED}\+: Triggered when the fingerprint features are extracted successfully.
\item {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+MATCH\+\_\+\+SUCCESS}\+: Triggered when a fingerprint match is successful.
\item {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+MATCH\+\_\+\+FAIL}\+: Triggered when a fingerprint mismatch occurs.
\item {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+ERROR}\+: Triggered for general errors during fingerprint processing.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function logs the corresponding message for each event. It can be modified or extended as needed for custom event handling in the application.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
To use this function in the application, assign it to the global event handler {\ttfamily g\+\_\+fingerprint\+\_\+event\+\_\+handler} in the {\ttfamily app\+\_\+main.\+c}.
\end{DoxyNote}

\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md14}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{5. Creating Custom High-\/\+Level Functions}{5. Creating Custom High-\/\+Level Functions}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md14}
This section explains how to extend the library by creating your own high-\/level functions using the mid-\/level command interface.\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md15}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{5.\+1 Mid-\/\+Level Command Functions}{5.\+1 Mid-\/\+Level Command Functions}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md15}
The library provides these key mid-\/level functions for direct module communication\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_aa621bd8222b32b5d2245f92e22934655}{fingerprint\+\_\+set\+\_\+command()}} -\/ Configures a command packet with parameters
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a25d10be1c372a32ba6e9ff2eb7cc60cb}{fingerprint\+\_\+send\+\_\+command()}} -\/ Transmits a command to the fingerprint module
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a0d5b756311c0909b7f123085fb54e5b5}{fingerprint\+\_\+calculate\+\_\+checksum()}} -\/ Computes the checksum for a packet
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a990dbb9f30ede2ef53091abceaca2667}{initialize\+\_\+event\+\_\+group()}} -\/ Creates an event group for synchronization
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_ad1328d8028e7288cb7edcd926e31d1b3}{cleanup\+\_\+event\+\_\+group()}} -\/ Cleans up the event group when finished
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md16}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{5.\+2 Creating a High-\/\+Level Function}{5.\+2 Creating a High-\/\+Level Function}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md16}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \#\# 6. Setting Up the Fingerprint Scanner This section provides a step-\/by-\/step guide for setting up and testing the ZW111 fingerprint scanner with the ESP32.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md19}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{6.\+1 Hardware Connections}{6.\+1 Hardware Connections}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md19}
Connect the fingerprint scanner to your ESP32 development board\+:

\tabulinesep=1mm
\begin{longtabu}spread 0pt [c]{*{2}{|X[-1]}|}
\hline
\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ Fingerprint Scanner   }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ ESP32    }\\\cline{1-2}
\endfirsthead
\hline
\endfoot
\hline
\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ Fingerprint Scanner   }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ ESP32    }\\\cline{1-2}
\endhead
VCC   &3.\+3V    \\\cline{1-2}
GND   &GND    \\\cline{1-2}
TX   &GPIO17 (RX)    \\\cline{1-2}
RX   &GPIO18 (TX)    \\\cline{1-2}
INT   &GPIO15   \\\cline{1-2}
\end{longtabu}


\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The default pins are GPIO5 for RX and GPIO6 for TX, but these can be changed using the {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a9d930710d85ff4f3085dd32e2ce89a8a}{fingerprint\+\_\+set\+\_\+pins()}} function. The INT pin is connected to GPIO15 and is used for interrupt-\/based finger detection.
\end{DoxyNote}

\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md21}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{6.\+3 Interrupt-\/\+Based Finger Detection}{6.\+3 Interrupt-\/\+Based Finger Detection}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md21}
The library automatically sets up interrupt-\/based finger detection using GPIO15. When a finger is placed on the sensor, the INT pin triggers an interrupt that\+:


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Detects finger placement with software debouncing
\item Signals the detection to a processing task
\item Automatically processes the finger based on the current operation mode
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

You can set the operation mode to control how finger detection is handled\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Set\ operation\ mode\ for\ verification}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{fingerprint_8h_a18d99335c54889f10f6ee774f35969de}{fingerprint\_set\_operation\_mode}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{fingerprint_8h_a7cc9a0fbe6e036dd6863cd96f416a68ca3f7842befa7b299dc3dc91a30462f093}{FINGER\_OP\_VERIFY}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Wait\ for\ a\ finger\ with\ timeout}}
\DoxyCodeLine{err\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{fingerprint_8h_a51b71265f769dca95a3075cec862b3ce}{fingerprint\_wait\_for\_finger}}(10000);\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 10\ second\ timeout}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (err\ ==\ ESP\_OK)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ESP\_LOGI(\mbox{\hyperlink{fingerprint_8c_afc3d101f633a076cc1ca84b85b6224b2}{TAG}},\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Finger\ detected\ and\ processed\ for\ verification"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md24}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{6.\+6 Troubleshooting}{6.\+6 Troubleshooting}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md24}
If you encounter issues\+:


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item {\bfseries{No response from scanner\+:}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Check power connections (3.\+3V/\+GND)
\item Verify TX/\+RX connections are correct and not swapped
\item Try a different baud rate
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Communication errors\+:}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure the TX/\+RX lines have pull-\/up resistors (typically 10kΩ)
\item Add delay between commands (v\+Task\+Delay(pd\+MS\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+TICKS(100)))
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{No finger detection interrupts\+:}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Check the INT pin connection to GPIO15
\item Verify INT pin is properly pulled down at rest
\item Test interrupt functioning using a GPIO test program
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Enrollment failures\+:}}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Clean both the sensor and the finger
\item Ensure consistent finger placement
\item Increase timeout values for enrollment operations 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_aadeaf43969208e0b520d8c6a2c974f9d}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!CHECKING\_LOCATION\_BIT@{CHECKING\_LOCATION\_BIT}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_aadeaf43969208e0b520d8c6a2c974f9d} 
\#define CHECKING\+\_\+\+LOCATION\+\_\+\+BIT~BIT2}



Event bit flag for checking if a fingerprint template location is available. 

This bit is set in the event group to indicate that the system is currently verifying whether a specified fingerprint template location is occupied.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Used in conjunction with {\ttfamily enroll\+\_\+event\+\_\+group} to synchronize location checking. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Packet ID indicating a command packet. 

The packet ID is a 1-\/byte value that defines the type of packet being sent.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0x01\+: Command packet
\item 0x02\+: Data packet

\item 0x04\+: End of data packet

This bit is set in the enroll\+\_\+event\+\_\+group when the fingerprint module\textquotesingle{}s information page has been successfully read and processed. \Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a68c7f0498bb1932350eb092be1b5e912}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!MAX\_PARAMETERS@{MAX\_PARAMETERS}}
\index{MAX\_PARAMETERS@{MAX\_PARAMETERS}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MAX\_PARAMETERS}{MAX\_PARAMETERS}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_a68c7f0498bb1932350eb092be1b5e912} 
\#define MAX\+\_\+\+PARAMETERS~256}



Maximum number of parameters supported in a fingerprint packet. 

Defines the fixed-\/size buffer for command-\/specific parameters in fingerprint communication. This value should be adjusted based on the largest expected parameter size to ensure sufficient space while maintaining efficient memory usage. Adjust based on the largest required parameter size. \Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a142810068f1b99cd93d3fc9f0e160e02}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!QUEUE\_SIZE@{QUEUE\_SIZE}}
\index{QUEUE\_SIZE@{QUEUE\_SIZE}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{QUEUE\_SIZE}{QUEUE\_SIZE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_a142810068f1b99cd93d3fc9f0e160e02} 
\#define QUEUE\+\_\+\+SIZE~64}



Defines the maximum number of fingerprint response packets in the queue. 

This value determines the capacity of {\ttfamily fingerprint\+\_\+response\+\_\+queue}, which stores fingerprint responses for asynchronous processing.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
A larger value increases buffering but consumes more memory. Adjust as needed based on system constraints. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a01cefd4d9668b7654e22cc46cfcee174}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!TEMPLATE\_UPLOAD\_COMPLETE\_BIT@{TEMPLATE\_UPLOAD\_COMPLETE\_BIT}}
\index{TEMPLATE\_UPLOAD\_COMPLETE\_BIT@{TEMPLATE\_UPLOAD\_COMPLETE\_BIT}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{TEMPLATE\_UPLOAD\_COMPLETE\_BIT}{TEMPLATE\_UPLOAD\_COMPLETE\_BIT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_a01cefd4d9668b7654e22cc46cfcee174} 
\#define TEMPLATE\+\_\+\+UPLOAD\+\_\+\+COMPLETE\+\_\+\+BIT~(1 $<$$<$ 3)}



Event bit indicating template upload has completed. 

This bit is set in the enroll\+\_\+event\+\_\+group when a template upload operation has successfully completed and all template data has been received. \Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a69d1c616ae544899c43fd1dbfcbaa086}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!UART\_READ\_TIMEOUT@{UART\_READ\_TIMEOUT}}
\index{UART\_READ\_TIMEOUT@{UART\_READ\_TIMEOUT}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UART\_READ\_TIMEOUT}{UART\_READ\_TIMEOUT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_a69d1c616ae544899c43fd1dbfcbaa086} 
\#define UART\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+TIMEOUT~100}



Timeout value for UART read operations. 

Defines the maximum wait time for receiving data over UART in milliseconds. Adjust this value based on the fingerprint module\textquotesingle{}s response time.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{fingerprint\_event\_handler\_t}{fingerprint\_event\_handler\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_a658eb2a1aea7e912aabef713b69d6789} 
typedef void(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} fingerprint\+\_\+event\+\_\+handler\+\_\+t) (\mbox{\hyperlink{structfingerprint__event__t}{fingerprint\+\_\+event\+\_\+t}} event)}



Typedef for the fingerprint event handler callback. 

This type is used to define a function pointer for handling fingerprint-\/related events. The function pointed to by the callback should take a single parameter of type {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5ae}{fingerprint\+\_\+event\+\_\+type\+\_\+t}}, representing the specific event that occurred.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em event} & The fingerprint event that occurred. This is an enumeration value of type {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5ae}{fingerprint\+\_\+event\+\_\+type\+\_\+t}}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5ae}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!fingerprint\_event\_type\_t@{fingerprint\_event\_type\_t}}
\index{fingerprint\_event\_type\_t@{fingerprint\_event\_type\_t}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{fingerprint\_event\_type\_t}{fingerprint\_event\_type\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5ae} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5ae}{fingerprint\+\_\+event\+\_\+type\+\_\+t}}}



Enum to define various fingerprint events. 

These events represent significant milestones or errors during the fingerprint processing. They allow for event-\/driven management of the fingerprint sensor actions.

Each event is triggered when a certain action or error occurs, making it easier for the application to respond to changes in the system state.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The event codes are used in an event handler system where functions can subscribe and react to specific events. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyEnumFields}[2]{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_NONE@{EVENT\_NONE}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_NONE@{EVENT\_NONE}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea939a6cc6d749a232a23ff324dca6d48c}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea939a6cc6d749a232a23ff324dca6d48c} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+NONE&Event representing no valid fingerprint event. This event is used as a default value when no other event is applicable. No event (Default value) \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_FINGER\_DETECTED@{EVENT\_FINGER\_DETECTED}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_FINGER\_DETECTED@{EVENT\_FINGER\_DETECTED}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea603fb16ec367104f40d98dea5d710e2b}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea603fb16ec367104f40d98dea5d710e2b} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+FINGER\+\_\+\+DETECTED&Event triggered when a fingerprint is detected on the sensor. This event occurs when the fingerprint module detects a finger placed on the sensor surface. It typically follows a successful FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+CMD\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+IMAGE operation.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This event indicates only that a finger is present on the sensor, not that a valid or good quality fingerprint image has been captured.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a4fa0db2c9622e0d4cbaa1e1c64c16364a9f79c8e7182bcc032acb0fab7f9215cc}{FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+OK} 

\doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aeafdbee660971b3da1a54885db913c82eb}{EVENT\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+FINGER\+\_\+\+DETECTED} Finger detected 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_IMAGE\_CAPTURED@{EVENT\_IMAGE\_CAPTURED}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_IMAGE\_CAPTURED@{EVENT\_IMAGE\_CAPTURED}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aeaeaeb81c0ee77f9345d3b965abc2387f9}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aeaeaeb81c0ee77f9345d3b965abc2387f9} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+IMAGE\+\_\+\+CAPTURED&Event triggered when the fingerprint module successfully captures an image. This event occurs after a FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+CMD\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+IMAGE command when the module successfully captures a valid fingerprint image that can be used for further processing.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
A successful image capture does not guarantee successful feature extraction. The quality of the captured image still needs to be sufficient for further operations.
\end{DoxyNote}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_FEATURE\_EXTRACTED@{EVENT\_FEATURE\_EXTRACTED}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_FEATURE\_EXTRACTED@{EVENT\_FEATURE\_EXTRACTED}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea1f5eb993d59aba8c41d37b86320efc1b}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea1f5eb993d59aba8c41d37b86320efc1b} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+EXTRACTED&Event triggered when fingerprint features are successfully extracted. This event occurs after executing the FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+CMD\+\_\+\+GEN\+\_\+\+CHAR command when the module successfully extracts characteristic features from the captured fingerprint image.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Feature extraction is a critical step in both enrollment and verification processes. A successful extraction indicates the image had sufficient quality for biometric processing.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a4c9c4a4e70842b49ce794917a355a0d7abdb8a3af0a2c53616968202e3af56e18}{FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+CMD\+\_\+\+GEN\+\_\+\+CHAR}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_MATCH\_FAIL@{EVENT\_MATCH\_FAIL}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_MATCH\_FAIL@{EVENT\_MATCH\_FAIL}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aeac16d33bd72e724f022d365db1ea16e63}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aeac16d33bd72e724f022d365db1ea16e63} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+MATCH\+\_\+\+FAIL&Event triggered when a fingerprint mismatch occurs. Occurs when no matching fingerprint is found in the database. Fingerprint mismatch \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_ERROR@{EVENT\_ERROR}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_ERROR@{EVENT\_ERROR}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aeaa45fa5ecff86270d410d4c89c527898a}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aeaa45fa5ecff86270d410d4c89c527898a} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+ERROR&Event triggered when a general error occurs during fingerprint processing. This event is a catch-\/all for various errors that may occur during fingerprint operations and don\textquotesingle{}t have more specific error events. It typically indicates an unexpected failure in command processing or hardware operation.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The event.\+status field contains the specific error code, and event.\+command indicates which command was being processed when the error occurred.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+ERROR General error 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_IMAGE\_FAIL@{EVENT\_IMAGE\_FAIL}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_IMAGE\_FAIL@{EVENT\_IMAGE\_FAIL}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea7ba4dbb06dfd6e55e77531a98e45382a}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea7ba4dbb06dfd6e55e77531a98e45382a} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+IMAGE\+\_\+\+FAIL&Event triggered when image capture fails. This event occurs when the fingerprint module is unable to capture a valid image from the sensor. This may happen if no finger is present, if the finger placement is poor, or if there are hardware issues with the image sensor.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This event corresponds to various status codes including FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+FINGER (0x02) or FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+IMAGE\+\_\+\+FAIL (0x03) depending on the specific cause.
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a4fa0db2c9622e0d4cbaa1e1c64c16364ab374faac8b33660ae02706b9e51e1609}{FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+IMAGE\+\_\+\+FAIL}

EVENT\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+EXTRACT\+\_\+\+FAIL&Event triggered when fingerprint feature extraction fails. This event occurs when the fingerprint module is unable to extract valid biometric features from the captured fingerprint image. This typically happens when the image quality is too poor, the finger placement is incorrect, or there is dirt or damage on the sensor surface.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This failure often requires capturing a new image with better finger placement or cleaning the finger/sensor before retrying.
\end{DoxyNote}

EVENT\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE\+\_\+\+RESTORED\+\_\+\+FAIL&Event triggered when fingerprint template restoration fails. Common status codes associated with this event include FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+FLASH\+\_\+\+RW\+\_\+\+ERROR, FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+DB\+\_\+\+RANGE\+\_\+\+ERROR or FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+PACKET\+\_\+\+ERROR.

EVENT\+\_\+\+LOW\+\_\+\+POWER\+\_\+\+MODE&Event triggered when the system enters low power mode. This event occurs after executing the FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+CMD\+\_\+\+SLEEP command when the fingerprint module successfully transitions to a low-\/power state to conserve energy. In this state, the module has reduced functionality until it is woken up.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
After this event, the module will not respond to most commands until it is woken up, typically by resetting the module or using a specific wake-\/up command if supported.
\end{DoxyNote}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_TEMPLATE\_LOADED@{EVENT\_TEMPLATE\_LOADED}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_TEMPLATE\_LOADED@{EVENT\_TEMPLATE\_LOADED}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea1bfcd0bdeec43f078a1031f6cccb8e78}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea1bfcd0bdeec43f078a1031f6cccb8e78} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE\+\_\+\+LOADED&Event triggered when a fingerprint template is successfully loaded from flash memory into the buffer. This event occurs after executing the {\ttfamily PS\+\_\+\+Load\+Char} command, indicating that the fingerprint template has been retrieved from the module’s internal storage and is now available for further operations such as matching, uploading, or storing in another location.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Ensure that the {\ttfamily PS\+\_\+\+Load\+Char} command completes successfully before relying on this event. If the template is corrupt or missing, subsequent operations like {\ttfamily PS\+\_\+\+Up\+Char} may return zeroed data.
\end{DoxyNote}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_SET\_CHIP\_ADDRESS\_SUCCESS@{EVENT\_SET\_CHIP\_ADDRESS\_SUCCESS}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_SET\_CHIP\_ADDRESS\_SUCCESS@{EVENT\_SET\_CHIP\_ADDRESS\_SUCCESS}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea28b68d343e7a6e364e6891cae4dc39fa}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea28b68d343e7a6e364e6891cae4dc39fa} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+CHIP\+\_\+\+ADDRESS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS&Event triggered when the chip address is successfully set. This event indicates that the FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+CMD\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+CHIP\+\_\+\+ADDR command was executed successfully and the module\textquotesingle{}s address has been updated. After this event, the module will only respond to commands sent to the new address.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
After changing the address, all subsequent commands must be sent to the new address or the module will not respond.
\end{DoxyNote}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_SET\_CHIP\_ADDRESS\_FAIL@{EVENT\_SET\_CHIP\_ADDRESS\_FAIL}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_SET\_CHIP\_ADDRESS\_FAIL@{EVENT\_SET\_CHIP\_ADDRESS\_FAIL}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aead281769970336ea3e27654aaf763480e}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aead281769970336ea3e27654aaf763480e} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+CHIP\+\_\+\+ADDRESS\+\_\+\+FAIL&Event triggered when setting the chip address fails. This event indicates that the FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+CMD\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+CHIP\+\_\+\+ADDR command failed to execute, possibly due to communication issues or invalid address values.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
When this event occurs, the module\textquotesingle{}s address remains unchanged and commands should continue to be sent to the original address.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a4c9c4a4e70842b49ce794917a355a0d7a65402541d63cf6dc14b0f717bdb1e50c}{FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+CMD\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+CHIP\+\_\+\+ADDR} 

\doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea28b68d343e7a6e364e6891cae4dc39fa}{EVENT\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+CHIP\+\_\+\+ADDRESS\+\_\+\+SUCCESS} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_PACKET\_RECEPTION\_FAIL@{EVENT\_PACKET\_RECEPTION\_FAIL}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_PACKET\_RECEPTION\_FAIL@{EVENT\_PACKET\_RECEPTION\_FAIL}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aeab8b82e7fb66cd086f6658b1ca0994343}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aeab8b82e7fb66cd086f6658b1ca0994343} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+PACKET\+\_\+\+RECEPTION\+\_\+\+FAIL&Event triggered when an attempt to receive a packet fails. This event occurs when there is a failure in receiving an expected data packet during multi-\/packet operations like template uploading or downloading. This typically indicates communication errors or protocol issues.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This event may be associated with various error codes including FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+PACKET\+\_\+\+ERROR (0x01) or FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+TIMEOUT (0x26).
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a4fa0db2c9622e0d4cbaa1e1c64c16364aafaf285f0d69ebf5d13978c7fddcc42d}{FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+PACKET\+\_\+\+ERROR} 

\doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea9f39a06e55c32b00c1d1dca7c88c1ced}{EVENT\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE\+\_\+\+UPLOADED} Failed to receive subsequent \doxylink{uniondata}{data} packets 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_ENROLLMENT\_COMPLETE@{EVENT\_ENROLLMENT\_COMPLETE}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_ENROLLMENT\_COMPLETE@{EVENT\_ENROLLMENT\_COMPLETE}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aeab449df3c72691894f10dfe66ac5e3e9a}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aeab449df3c72691894f10dfe66ac5e3e9a} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+ENROLLMENT\+\_\+\+COMPLETE&Event triggered when a fingerprint is successfully enrolled. This event occurs when the complete enrollment process (multiple image captures, feature extraction, template generation and storage) completes successfully. The event data contains enrollment details including the template ID, number of attempts required, and whether a duplicate was found.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The enrollment\+\_\+info structure in the event data contains the template\+\_\+id, is\+\_\+duplicate flag, and attempts count fields with detailed enrollment information.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
fingerprint\+\_\+data.\+enrollment\+\_\+info 

\doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a4fa0db2c9622e0d4cbaa1e1c64c16364a9f79c8e7182bcc032acb0fab7f9215cc}{FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+OK} 

\doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea7c87467c0dd84a2f0f43adc6dc921f24}{EVENT\+\_\+\+ENROLLMENT\+\_\+\+FAIL} Fingerprint enrollment process completed 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{EVENT\_ENROLLMENT\_FAIL@{EVENT\_ENROLLMENT\_FAIL}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!EVENT\_ENROLLMENT\_FAIL@{EVENT\_ENROLLMENT\_FAIL}}}\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea7c87467c0dd84a2f0f43adc6dc921f24}\label{fingerprint_8h_a6a07f45ee6da95e2ccbcbb0e0699f5aea7c87467c0dd84a2f0f43adc6dc921f24} 
EVENT\+\_\+\+ENROLLMENT\+\_\+\+FAIL&Event triggered when a fingerprint enrollment process fails. This event occurs when the enrollment process cannot be completed due to issues such as poor fingerprint quality, inconsistent placement, or internal errors in the fingerprint module.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The enrollment\+\_\+info structure in the event data still contains information about the failed enrollment attempt, including the number of attempts made.
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a7b34c403a57b0b6db25994554ae7fe98}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!enroll\_fingerprint@{enroll\_fingerprint}}
\index{enroll\_fingerprint@{enroll\_fingerprint}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enroll\_fingerprint()}{enroll\_fingerprint()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_a7b34c403a57b0b6db25994554ae7fe98} 
esp\+\_\+err\+\_\+t enroll\+\_\+fingerprint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{location}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Performs manual fingerprint enrollment at a specified storage location. 

This function executes a step-\/by-\/step fingerprint enrollment process, handling user interaction and ensuring proper fingerprint capture and storage at the given location.\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md39}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Enrollment Process\+:}{Enrollment Process\+:}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md39}

\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Wait for a finger to be placed on the scanner ({\ttfamily PS\+\_\+\+Get\+Image}).
\item If a fingerprint is detected, generate the first fingerprint template ({\ttfamily PS\+\_\+\+Gen\+Char1}).
\item Prompt the user to remove their finger and wait for confirmation of removal.
\item Once the finger is removed, wait for the same finger to be placed again.
\item Capture the fingerprint again ({\ttfamily PS\+\_\+\+Get\+Image}) and generate the second template ({\ttfamily PS\+\_\+\+Gen\+Char2}).
\item Merge both templates into a single fingerprint model ({\ttfamily PS\+\_\+\+Reg\+Model}).
\item Store the fingerprint template in the fingerprint module’s database at the specified {\ttfamily location} ({\ttfamily PS\+\_\+\+Store\+Char}).
\end{DoxyEnumerate}\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md40}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Error Handling\+:}{Error Handling\+:}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md40}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If a finger is not detected within the allowed retries, the function will return an error.
\item If the finger is not removed within a timeout period, the process will restart.
\item If enrollment fails at any step, it retries up to three times before failing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function does not run as a Free\+RTOS task but can be called from one. It dynamically creates an event group for synchronization and deletes it upon completion.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em location} & The storage location (ID) where the fingerprint template will be saved.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily ESP\+\_\+\+OK} if fingerprint enrollment is successful.
\item {\ttfamily ESP\+\_\+\+FAIL} if enrollment fails after the maximum number of attempts.
\item {\ttfamily ESP\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+MEM} if memory allocation for the event group fails. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a2fed032ecaed7d5e40172733dc09d4ca}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!extract\_packet\_from\_raw\_data@{extract\_packet\_from\_raw\_data}}

\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a759d58795c9a87a5d2fa233e52e5d580}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!fingerprint\_init@{fingerprint\_init}}
\index{fingerprint\_init@{fingerprint\_init}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{fingerprint\_init()}{fingerprint\_init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_a759d58795c9a87a5d2fa233e52e5d580} 
esp\+\_\+err\+\_\+t fingerprint\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initializes the fingerprint scanner module. 

This function sets up the UART interface, configures the necessary pins, installs the UART driver, and checks for the power-\/on handshake signal (0x55). If the handshake is not received, it waits for 200ms before proceeding. It also initializes a Free\+RTOS queue for response handling and creates a background task to continuously read responses.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ESP\+\_\+\+OK if initialization is successful.
\item ESP\+\_\+\+FAIL if queue creation or task creation fails.
\item UART-\/related errors if UART initialization fails. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a86bbdf25b64da0def2418a308fbc81cf}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!fingerprint\_read\_response@{fingerprint\_read\_response}}
\index{fingerprint\_read\_response@{fingerprint\_read\_response}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{fingerprint\_read\_response()}{fingerprint\_read\_response()}}

Reads the response packet from UART and returns a dynamically allocated \doxylink{struct_fingerprint_packet}{Fingerprint\+Packet}. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The caller is responsible for freeing the allocated memory using {\ttfamily free()} after processing the response to avoid memory leaks.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Pointer to the received \doxylink{struct_fingerprint_packet}{Fingerprint\+Packet}, or NULL on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_aa621bd8222b32b5d2245f92e22934655}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!fingerprint\_set\_command@{fingerprint\_set\_command}}
\index{fingerprint\_set\_command@{fingerprint\_set\_command}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{fingerprint\_set\_command()}{fingerprint\_set\_command()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_aa621bd8222b32b5d2245f92e22934655} 
esp\+\_\+err\+\_\+t fingerprint\+\_\+set\+\_\+command (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_fingerprint_packet}{Fingerprint\+Packet}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{cmd}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{command}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{params}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{param\+\_\+length}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initializes or updates a fingerprint command packet. 

This function modifies an existing {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_fingerprint_packet}{Fingerprint\+Packet}} structure to prepare a command before sending it to the fingerprint sensor. It ensures that the parameter length does not exceed the allowed size and automatically computes the checksum.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
This function {\bfseries{modifies}} the provided {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_fingerprint_packet}{Fingerprint\+Packet}} structure in-\/place. Developers should ensure that any previous data in the structure is not needed before calling this function, unless they create a {\bfseries{new}} {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_fingerprint_packet}{Fingerprint\+Packet}} instance.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em cmd} & Pointer to the {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_fingerprint_packet}{Fingerprint\+Packet}} to be modified. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em command} & Command byte to be set in the packet. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em params} & Pointer to a parameter array (can be NULL if no parameters). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em param\+\_\+length} & Number of parameters (max {\ttfamily MAX\+\_\+\+PARAMETERS}). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily ESP\+\_\+\+OK} on success.
\item {\ttfamily ESP\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+ARG} if {\ttfamily cmd} is NULL.
\item {\ttfamily ESP\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+SIZE} if {\ttfamily param\+\_\+length} exceeds {\ttfamily MAX\+\_\+\+PARAMETERS}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function does not allocate new memory. The caller is responsible for managing {\ttfamily cmd}. If modification of an existing {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_fingerprint_packet}{Fingerprint\+Packet}} is not desired, a {\bfseries{new instance}} should be created before calling this function. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_ac22bc43cb5b4e21246c6dbf734e6d919}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!fingerprint\_status\_event\_handler@{fingerprint\_status\_event\_handler}}
\index{fingerprint\_status\_event\_handler@{fingerprint\_status\_event\_handler}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{fingerprint\_status\_event\_handler()}{fingerprint\_status\_event\_handler()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_ac22bc43cb5b4e21246c6dbf734e6d919} 
void fingerprint\+\_\+status\+\_\+event\+\_\+handler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{fingerprint_8h_a4fa0db2c9622e0d4cbaa1e1c64c16364}{fingerprint\+\_\+status\+\_\+t}}}]{status}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_fingerprint_packet}{Fingerprint\+Packet}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{packet}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Handles fingerprint status events and triggers corresponding high-\/level events. 

This function processes status codes received from the fingerprint module and maps them to predefined high-\/level fingerprint events. These events help notify the application about the outcome of fingerprint operations.

The following status codes and their corresponding events are handled\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+OK} → {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+FINGER\+\_\+\+DETECTED}
\item {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+FINGER} → {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+IMAGE\+\_\+\+CAPTURED}
\item {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+IMAGE\+\_\+\+FAIL}, {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+DRY}, {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+WET}, {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+CHAOTIC}, {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+UPLOAD\+\_\+\+IMAGE\+\_\+\+FAIL}, {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+IMAGE\+\_\+\+AREA\+\_\+\+SMALL}, {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+IMAGE\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+AVAILABLE} → {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+IMAGE\+\_\+\+FAIL}
\item {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+FEW\+\_\+\+POINTS} → {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+EXTRACT\+\_\+\+FAIL}
\item {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+MISMATCH}, {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+FOUND} → {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+MATCH\+\_\+\+FAIL}
\item {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+DB\+\_\+\+FULL} → {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+DB\+\_\+\+FULL}
\item {\ttfamily FINGERPRINT\+\_\+\+TIMEOUT} → {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+ERROR}
\item Various sensor operation failures → {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+SENSOR\+\_\+\+ERROR}
\item Other unexpected statuses → {\ttfamily EVENT\+\_\+\+ERROR}
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em status} & The fingerprint status received from the sensor. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_adb364663a6f8cf989e0a0c055dc49de2}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!read\_response\_task@{read\_response\_task}}
\index{read\_response\_task@{read\_response\_task}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{read\_response\_task()}{read\_response\_task()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_adb364663a6f8cf989e0a0c055dc49de2} 
void read\+\_\+response\+\_\+task (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pv\+Parameter}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Task to continuously read fingerprint responses from UART. 

This Free\+RTOS task reads fingerprint sensor responses and enqueues them into the response queue for further processing. It runs indefinitely, ensuring that responses are captured asynchronously.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pv\+Parameter} & Unused parameter (NULL by default).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The function reads responses using {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a86bbdf25b64da0def2418a308fbc81cf}{fingerprint\+\_\+read\+\_\+response()}}, validates them, and sends them to {\ttfamily fingerprint\+\_\+response\+\_\+queue}. If the queue is full, the response is dropped with a warning log.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
This task should be created only once during initialization and should not be terminated unexpectedly, as it ensures continuous response handling. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_af73611117782f343652a3693d257e951}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!verify\_fingerprint@{verify\_fingerprint}}
\index{verify\_fingerprint@{verify\_fingerprint}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{verify\_fingerprint()}{verify\_fingerprint()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_af73611117782f343652a3693d257e951} 
esp\+\_\+err\+\_\+t verify\+\_\+fingerprint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Verifies a fingerprint by capturing an image, extracting features, and searching in the database. 

This function attempts to verify a fingerprint up to a maximum number of attempts. It captures a fingerprint image, processes it, and searches for a match in the database. If a match is found, the function returns ESP\+\_\+\+OK; otherwise, it returns ESP\+\_\+\+FAIL after all attempts.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ESP\+\_\+\+OK if the fingerprint matches an entry in the database.
\item ESP\+\_\+\+FAIL if verification fails after the maximum attempts.
\item ESP\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+MEM if the event group could not be created. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}


\doxysubsection{Variable Documentation}
\Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_aeb4fc4aba1a22ae72ee5746099c3a18e}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!enroll\_event\_group@{enroll\_event\_group}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enroll\_event\_group}{enroll\_event\_group}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_aeb4fc4aba1a22ae72ee5746099c3a18e} 
Event\+Group\+Handle\+\_\+t enroll\+\_\+event\+\_\+group = NULL\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Event group handle for fingerprint enrollment status. 

This Free\+RTOS event group is used to synchronize fingerprint enrollment operations by setting event bits based on success or failure. \Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a16f6ad612675010ed65702c824b3d167}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!enrollment\_in\_progress@{enrollment\_in\_progress}}
\index{enrollment\_in\_progress@{enrollment\_in\_progress}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enrollment\_in\_progress}{enrollment\_in\_progress}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_a16f6ad612675010ed65702c824b3d167} 
bool enrollment\+\_\+in\+\_\+progress\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Indicates whether an enrollment process is currently in progress. 

This external boolean variable is used to track the state of the fingerprint enrollment process. When {\ttfamily true}, it signifies that the enrollment process is ongoing. When {\ttfamily false}, it indicates that no enrollment is currently taking place. \Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_ac1bc88ca9eeff4bcae8ac419f8653c07}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!g\_fingerprint\_event\_handler@{g\_fingerprint\_event\_handler}}
\index{g\_fingerprint\_event\_handler@{g\_fingerprint\_event\_handler}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{g\_fingerprint\_event\_handler}{g\_fingerprint\_event\_handler}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_ac1bc88ca9eeff4bcae8ac419f8653c07} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{fingerprint_8h_a658eb2a1aea7e912aabef713b69d6789}{fingerprint\+\_\+event\+\_\+handler\+\_\+t}} g\+\_\+fingerprint\+\_\+event\+\_\+handler\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Global pointer to the fingerprint event handler function. 

This pointer is used to assign a function that will handle fingerprint-\/related events. The function should be defined by the user and should match the {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_a658eb2a1aea7e912aabef713b69d6789}{fingerprint\+\_\+event\+\_\+handler\+\_\+t}} callback type. The event handler is called whenever a fingerprint-\/related event occurs, such as detection, image capture, or match results. \Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a14662050a710495e6c9125a02ee17fd5}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!PS\_AutoEnroll@{PS\_AutoEnroll}}

Automatically enrolls a fingerprint template. 

This packet structure should be overwritten using {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_aa621bd8222b32b5d2245f92e22934655}{fingerprint\+\_\+set\+\_\+command()}} because its parameters (ID number, number of entries, and additional settings) are dynamic and depend on the user\textquotesingle{}s choice.\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md27}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Parameters\+:}{Parameters\+:}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md27}

Performs a handshake with the fingerprint module. 

Used to verify communication with the fingerprint module. \Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_aeb574ccc855812d08218c92966c6ea59}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!PS\_LoadChar@{PS\_LoadChar}}
\index{PS\_LoadChar@{PS\_LoadChar}!fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{PS\_LoadChar}{PS\_LoadChar}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{fingerprint_8h_aeb574ccc855812d08218c92966c6ea59} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_fingerprint_packet}{Fingerprint\+Packet}} PS\+\_\+\+Load\+Char\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Loads a fingerprint template from flash memory into the module\textquotesingle{}s buffer. 

This command instructs the fingerprint module to retrieve a stored fingerprint template from the flash database and load it into a specified template buffer.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The {\ttfamily parameters} field should be set before use\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily parameters\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}} = Buffer ID (target buffer)
\item {\ttfamily parameters\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}} = High byte of Page ID
\item {\ttfamily parameters\mbox{[}2\mbox{]}} = Low byte of Page ID
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The checksum must be recalculated before sending the packet. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Performs an immediate fingerprint search in the database. 

This packet structure should be overwritten using {\ttfamily \doxylink{fingerprint_8h_aa621bd8222b32b5d2245f92e22934655}{fingerprint\+\_\+set\+\_\+command()}} because its parameters (Start Page, Number of Pages) are dynamic.\hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md36}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Parameters\+:}{Parameters\+:}}\label{fingerprint_8h_autotoc_md36}

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_fingerprint_packet}{Fingerprint\+Packet}} PS\+\_\+\+Up\+Char\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Uploads a stored fingerprint template from the module. 

Upload template from buffer to main control.

This command uploads the fingerprint template stored in the buffer to the main control unit. The function is supported when the encryption level is set to 0. \Hypertarget{fingerprint_8h_a8d25f5cf1e5e1c6b6415485947add3d6}\index{fingerprint.h@{fingerprint.h}!PS\_Uplmage@{PS\_Uplmage}}
